3311

PUBLIC NOTICE
At the General Body Meeting of SIDDHA SAMAJ, held at Vatakara Siddha Samaj Head Office (Siddhasramam,
Vatakara). On 29th September 2014, As per Section 222 of Siddha Samaj Rules Brahmasri S. Bhakthavatsalan has been
elected as the new General Representative of Siddha Samaj in the place of Brahmasri S. Dhruvan, the then General
Representative since Siddha Samaj on 2nd October 2014.
It is, therefore notified to all that since 2nd October 2014 onwards the whole authority and liability of General
Representative with respect to Siddha Samaj, assets, etc., as per Siddha Samaj, Rules, is vested with the said
at Brahmasri S. Bhakthavatsalan.
S. ARUNAGIRI NATHAN,
General Secretary.
For Siddha Samaj
S. SREENIVASAN,
(General President).
Siddhasramam, Ammampalayam,
Salem-636 141,
29th October 2014.

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
